Use patient zip code to find the county the patient lives in by going to https://www.unitedstateszipcodes.org/. Enter the zip code in the main text field and use the associated county on the right side of the result field. Go to https://www2.census.gov/programs-surveys/acs/data/covid_19/Data_Profiles_for_HHS/050-County_By_State/. Select the dp02_XX.csv file where XX = the two letter abbreviation for the appropriate state. On row 166 find the total population for the appropriate county.  If the total population is <2,500 enter a value of "Rural Population"; if 2,500 - 50,000 enter a value of "Urban Cluster"; or if >50,000 enter "Urban Population"

IMMUNOSUPPRESSION: TEXT | The indicator that describes whether or not immunosuppressive therapy was administered.
MEDICALLY_UNDERSERVED_AREA: TEXT | Areas or populations designated by HRSA as having too few primary care providers, high infant mortality, high poverty or a high elderly population:  Use patient zip code to find the county the patient lives in by going to https://www.unitedstateszipcodes.org/ - enter the zip code in the main text field and use the associated county on the right side of the result field. Go to data.hrsa.gov website and select "Query Data". Pick the Medically Underserved Areas/Populations (MUA/P) data source in the step 1 menu and select "View Data". Enter the name of the county (_______ county) in the first "Service Area" column, adding the state in the 5th column may help direct you to the data.  If the designation type in the third column is "medically underserved area" enter "Yes" as the value. If the county generates a "No data available in table" enter "No" as the value.  A value of "Unknown" indicates that sufficient data was not available to look up the value.  If value is yes, complete the Medically_underserved_score d
KNOWN_GENETIC_PREDISPOSITION_MUTATION: TEXT | A yes/no/unknown indicator to identify whether there is a known genetic predisposition mutation present in the patient.
COVID19_COMPLICATIONS_SEVERITY: TEXT | Text term that retrospectively indicates the worst complications during COVID-19 infectious disorder in the patient.
CANCER_INCIDENCE: TEXT | Incidence of specific cancer type in a defined area (a number between 0 and 100). The rate of incident cases per population of 100,000 persons of a specific type of cancer as designated in the "primary_diagnosis" data element in the county where the patient resides, using the most recent 2013-2017 NCI Cancer Atlas derived data.  Use patient zip code to find the county the patient lives in by going to https://www.unitedstateszipcodes.org/. Enter the zip code in the main text field and use the asociated county on the right side of the result field. On the https://gis.cancer.gov/canceratlas/tableview/ website, choose "Incidence" from the Topic dropdown menu, state of interest from the Area menu, "All Races" from the Race menu, and the cancer type ("Both Sexes" when possible) from the Statistic menu. Find the county of interest and enter the numeric Age-Adjusted Rate per 100,000 as the value.

## HTAN_VERSIONED.SCRNASEQ_MSK_SCLC_EPITHELIAL_CELLS_R3
feature_name: TEXT | Gene name from HUGO Human Gene Nomenclature Committee (https://www.genenames.org/)
is_primary_data: BOOLEAN | Indicates if the sample is primary or not (True/False)
SCLC_subtype_plus_TP53_RB1_wt: TEXT | SCLC subtype plus a label for the TP53/RB1 wild-type SCLC
suspension_type: TEXT | Cell, nucleus, or na, as corresponding to sample preparation
feature_biotype: TEXT | Biological type of feature (e.g. gene)
treatment: TEXT | The type of treatment recieved by the patient
iObs: NUMBER | Index to cell barcodes
MHCII_PRESENTATION: FLOAT | Gene signature score for MHCII presentation
tissue_ontology_term_id: TEXT | Uber-anatomy ontology ID (REF: https://www.ebi.ac.uk/ols/ontologies/uberon) (ex.UBERON:2001190)
sex_ontology_term_id: TEXT | Phenotype And Trait Ontology ID, PATO:0000384 for male, PATO:0000383 for female, or unknown if unavailable
assay: TEXT | An assay based on 10X Genomics. Example : 100x3’ v2
total_counts: FLOAT | Total number of gene expression counts (or UMIs mapped) for a given cell
tissue: TEXT | Derived from UBERON or CL terms that best describes the tissue that the cell was derived from.
development_stage: TEXT | Human development stage derived from HsapDv term  (Example if data is Homo sapiens, development stage is obtained from Link. HsapDv:0000114 - 20-year-old human stage)
histo: TEXT | Type of cancer, only SCLC
assay_ontology_term_id: TEXT | Experimental Factor Ontology ID (REF: https://www.ebi.ac.uk/ols/ontologies/efo)
treatment_categorized: TEXT | Treatment category, includes TMZ,camptothecin,Chemo_1L,TMZ,Chemo_1L,IO_2L,Naive,ChemoIO_1L
donor_id: TEXT | Identifies a unique individual that data were derived from
MHCI_PRESENTATION: FLOAT | Gene signature score for MHCI presentation
clusters_fine: TEXT | The fine grained cluster labels placed on each cell, relates to cell subtypes.
batch: TEXT | Sample ID
NEUROD_genes: FLOAT | Average expression of all NEUROD genes
cell_type_ontology_term_id: TEXT | Cell Ontology ID (i.e. CL:0000784)  (REF: https://www.ebi.ac.uk/ols/ontologies/cl)
procedure: TEXT | The method used in sampling the tumor, Biopsy, Resection, or Thoracentesis
feature_is_filtered: BOOLEAN | Indicates if the feature (gene) was/should be filtered in analysis
pval_SCLC_P: FLOAT | p-value for calling sample SCLC_P
mito_frac: FLOAT | Percent of UMIs mapping to mitochondrial genes
development_stage_ontology_term_id: TEXT | Human Developmental Stages ID (REF: https://www.ebi.ac.uk/ols/ontologies/hsapdv) or Mouse Developmental Stages ID (REF: https://www.ebi.ac.uk/ols/ontologies/mmusdv) (HsapDv if human, MmusDv if mouse, unknown if information unavailable)
RBP_frac: FLOAT | Percent of UMIs mapping to RNA-binding proteins (RBPs)
X_value: FLOAT | Expression value for a given gene and cell
pval_SCLC_A: FLOAT | p-value for calling sample SCLC_A
log1p_n_genes_by_counts: FLOAT | Log (N+1) on the number of genes per cell
log1p_total_counts: FLOAT | Log (N+1) on the number of gene expression counts (UMIs mapped) for a given cell
pval_SCLC_N: FLOAT | p-value for calling sample SCLC_N
disease_ontology_term_id: TEXT | MONDO disease ontology ID (REF: https://www.ebi.ac.uk/ols/ontologies/mondo) (ex. MONDO:0100426 or PATO:0000461 for 'normal')
n_genes_by_counts: FLOAT | Number of genes detected in a given cell
HTAN_Participant_ID: TEXT | HTAN ID associated with a patient based on HTAN ID SOP (eg HTANx_yyy )
feature_reference: TEXT | A reference to the feature: NCBI Taxonomy ID
HTAN_Biospecimen_ID: TEXT | HTAN ID associated with a biosample based on HTAN ID SOP (eg HTANx_yyy_zzz)
self_reported_ethnicity: TEXT | Ethnicity of the individual (obtained from HANCESTRO terms for Homo sapiens)
iVar: NUMBER | Index to gene IDs
disease: TEXT | Description of disease (example: lung adenocarcinoma) or normal cells
recurrent_cluster: BOOLEAN | Whether it belongs to the PLCG2-high recurrent cluster
SCLC_subtype: TEXT | SCLC subtype
cell_type: TEXT | The type of cell (i.e. T-cell)
sex: TEXT | Phenotypic sex
organism_ontology_term_id: TEXT | NCBITaxon ID (REF: https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/taxonomy) (ex. NCBITaxon:9606 for human, NCBITaxon:10090 for mouse)
self_reported_ethnicity_ontology_term_id: TEXT | If human, the Human Ancestry Ontology ID (i.e. HANCESTRO:0005) (REF: https://www.ebi.ac.uk/ols/ontologies/hancestro); "multiethnic" if more than one ethnicity. "Unknown" if human and no information, else "na" if non-human
clusters: NUMBER | The coarse grained cluster labels placed on each cell, relates to cell type and state.
organism: TEXT | The genus and species from which biosamples are derived
SCLC_major_subtype_of_sample: TEXT | Major SCLC subtype of the sample

eccentricity: FLOAT | Eccentricity of the ellipse that has the same second-moments as the region, returned as a scalar. The eccentricity is the ratio of the distance between the foci of the ellipse and its major axis length. The value is between 0 and 1. (0 and 1 are degenerate cases. An ellipse whose eccentricity is 0 is actually a circle, while an ellipse whose eccentricity is 1 is a line segment.)

CD36status: NUMBER | Presence (1) or absence (0) of the given marker as described in https://doi.org/10.1016/j.cell.2021.12.031

myoep_dist_MaxDist: FLOAT | Maximum distance from cell centroid to perimeter location of myoepithelial mask
Neighbor_dist_TUMOR: FLOAT | Mean prevalence of given cell phenotype within a 36 micrometer radius of the index cell
duct_core_mask: NUMBER | Presence (1) or absence (0) of the specified mask marker as described in https://doi.org/10.1016/j.cell.2021.12.023
Neighbor_dist_MACS: FLOAT | Mean prevalence of given cell phenotype within a 36 micrometer radius of the index cell

## HTAN_VERSIONED.SCHEMA_R2
Valid_Values: TEXT | The range of attribute X: the values that can be assigned to attribute X; these values can include/be other attributes (i.e. listed in the 'Attribute' columns) themselves. Comma separated. If none provided any non-null value is valid for attribute X.
Validation_Rules: TEXT | What type of data is allowed in the Valid Values column. Only relevant if Valid Values are not present in the row. E.g. string, list, integer
DependsOn: TEXT | Important characteristics, if any, of attribute X that need to be recorded as metadata features given attribute X is specified. These characteristics could be attributes or properties of attributes (i.e. they are listed in the 'Attribute' column and/or under the "Properties" column). Comma separated.
DependsOn_Component: TEXT | Each component is a high level ontology class in which entities/objects are categorized/componentized; a component is an entity on its own that needs to be defined in the schema
Parent: TEXT | Parent class of this attribute - i.e. where to "hook" this attribute into an existing schema. Note that this assumes a single existing schema/a single json-ld schema context; if we need to support classes/attributes/properties defined across multiple schemas/json-ld contexts we'd need to add a schema/context column that specifies the context of each attribute, if different from the context of the attribute's parent.
Required: TEXT | Indicate if specifying value for attribute X is mandatory or optional by default. Set to TRUE or FALSE. If TRUE, a data contributor must provide a value for attribute X (e.g. one of the valid values in 'Valid Values', if any are specified). If FALSE, a data contributor may select between 'Not Applicable' or 'Not Specified' as a value for attribute X. Note that an attribute may not be required by default (i.e. 'Required' is set to FALSE), but it could be required by virtue of being an attribute of another required attribute (e.g. see ERCC).
Attribute: TEXT | Key characteristic X of the assay, related protocol, or downstream data that we want to record as metadata feature.
Description: TEXT | Provide a definition or a reference containing the definition of attribute X. Preferably provide a source ontology link or code in addition to the definition. Leave blank if the final description is pending.
Source: TEXT | The source for the description of the term, usually an URI. Ontologies can be used as sources. E.g. Library Construction Method has source: http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/OBI_0000711
Properties: TEXT | Properties specific to a particular attribute; note that properties could be attributes themselves (i.e. listed under the "Attributes" column).

pSTAT1: FLOAT | Mean intensity of pixels for specified marker

## HTAN_VERSIONED.SCHEMA_R3
Required: TEXT | Indicate if specifying value for attribute X is mandatory or optional by default. Set to TRUE or FALSE. If TRUE, a data contributor must provide a value for attribute X (e.g. one of the valid values in 'Valid Values', if any are specified). If FALSE, a data contributor may select between 'Not Applicable' or 'Not Specified' as a value for attribute X. Note that an attribute may not be required by default (i.e. 'Required' is set to FALSE), but it could be required by virtue of being an attribute of another required attribute (e.g. see ERCC).
DependsOn_Component: TEXT | Each component is a high level ontology class in which entities/objects are categorized/componentized; a component is an entity on its own that needs to be defined in the schema
Validation_Rules: TEXT | What type of data is allowed in the Valid Values column. Only relevant if Valid Values are not present in the row. E.g. string, list, integer
Properties: TEXT | Properties specific to a particular attribute; note that properties could be attributes themselves (i.e. listed under the 'Attributes' column).
Attribute: TEXT | Key characteristic X of the assay, related protocol, or downstream data that we want to record as metadata feature.
Parent: TEXT | Parent class of this attribute - i.e. where to 'hook' this attribute into an existing schema. Note that this assumes a single existing schema/a single json-ld schema context; if we need to support classes/attributes/properties defined across multiple schemas/json-ld contexts we'd need to add a schema/context column that specifies the context of each attribute, if different from the context of the attribute's parent.
DependsOn: TEXT | Important characteristics, if any, of attribute X that need to be recorded as metadata features given attribute X is specified. These characteristics could be attributes or properties of attributes (i.e. they are listed in the 'Attribute' column and/or under the 'Properties' column). Comma separated.
Source: TEXT | The source for the description of the term, usually an URI. Ontologies can be used as sources. E.g. Library Construction Method has source: http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/OBI_0000711
Valid_Values: TEXT | The range of attribute X: the values that can be assigned to attribute X; these values can include/be other attributes (i.e. listed in the 'Attribute' columns) themselves. Comma separated. If none provided any non-null value is valid for attribute X.
Description: TEXT | Provide a definition or a reference containing the definition of attribute X. Preferably provide a source ontology link or code in addition to the definition. Leave blank if the final description is pending.

## HTAN_VERSIONED.SCHEMA_R5
SOURCE: TEXT | The source for the description of the term, usually an URI. Ontologies can be used as sources. E.g. Library Construction Method has source: http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/OBI_0000711
DEPENDSON: TEXT | Important characteristics, if any, of attribute X that need to be recorded as metadata features given attribute X is specified. These characteristics could be attributes or properties of attributes (i.e. they are listed in the 'Attribute' column and/or under the 'Properties' column). Comma separated.
DESCRIPTION: TEXT | Provide a definition or a reference containing the definition of attribute X. Preferably provide a source ontology link or code in addition to the definition. Leave blank if the final description is pending.
REQUIRED: TEXT | Indicate if specifying value for attribute X is mandatory or optional by default. Set to TRUE or FALSE. If TRUE, a data contributor must provide a value for attribute X (e.g. one of the valid values in 'Valid Values', if any are specified). If FALSE, a data contributor may select between 'Not Applicable' or 'Not Specified' as a value for attribute X. Note that an attribute may not be required by default (i.e. 'Required' is set to FALSE), but it could be required by virtue of being an attribute of another required attribute (e.g. see ERCC).
DEPENDSON_COMPONENT: TEXT | Each component is a high level ontology class in which entities/objects are categorized/componentized; a component is an entity on its own that needs to be defined in the schema
ATTRIBUTE: TEXT | Key characteristic X of the assay, related protocol, or downstream data that we want to record as metadata feature.
VALIDATION_RULES: TEXT | What type of data is allowed in the Valid Values column. Only relevant if Valid Values are not present in the row. E.g. string, list, integer
PROPERTIES: TEXT | Properties specific to a particular attribute; note that properties could be attributes themselves (i.e. listed under the 'Attributes' column).
VALID_VALUES: TEXT | The range of attribute X: the values that can be assigned to attribute X; these values can include/be other attributes (i.e. listed in the 'Attribute' columns) themselves. Comma separated. If none provided any non-null value is valid for attribute X.
PARENT: TEXT | Parent class of this attribute - i.e. where to 'hook' this attribute into an existing schema. Note that this assumes a single existing schema/a single json-ld schema context; if we need to support classes/attributes/properties defined across multiple schemas/json-ld contexts we'd need to add a schema/context column that specifies the context of each attribute, if different from the context of the attribute's parent.

Gene_Symbol: TEXT | The text term used to describe a gene targeted or included in molecular analysis. For rearrangements, this is should be used to represent the reference gene. Note: This node is meant to capture molecular tests that were completed clinically for the participant and only includes data from diagnostic array that was completed prior to research sequencing was done. Do not include data related to research assay outputs here.
Treatment_Type: TEXT | Text term that describes the kind of treatment administered.
Site_of_Resection_or_Biopsy: TEXT | The text term used to describe the anatomic site of the resection or biopsy of the patient's malignant disease, as described by the World Health Organization's (WHO) International Classification of Diseases for Oncology (ICD-O).
Progression_or_Recurrence: TEXT | Yes/No/unknown indicator to identify whether a patient has had a new tumor event after initial treatment.
Manifest_Id: TEXT | Synapse ID of manifest containing file annotation
Test_Result: TEXT | The text term used to describe the result of the molecular test. If the test result was a numeric value see test_value. Note: This node is meant to capture molecular tests that were completed clinically for the participant and only includes data from diagnostic array that was completed prior to research sequencing was done. Do not include data related to research assay outputs here.
Rural_vs_Urban: TEXT | Density of population in the county of residence, based on census data (updated last on 4/28/20). Use patient zip code to find the county the patient lives in by going to https://www.unitedstateszipcodes.org/. Enter the zip code in the main text field and use the associated county on the right side of the result field. Go to https://www2.census.gov/programs-surveys/acs/data/covid_19/Data_Profiles_for_HHS/050-County_By_State/. Select the dp02_XX.csv file where XX = the two letter abbreviation for the appropriate state. On row 166 find the total population for the appropriate county.  If the total population is <2,500 enter a value of "Rural Population"; if 2,500 - 50,000 enter a value of "Urban Cluster"; or if >50,000 enter "Urban Population"
Age_at_Diagnosis: TEXT | Age at the time of diagnosis expressed in number of days since birth.
Molecular_Analysis_Method: TEXT | The text term used to describe the method used for molecular analysis. Note: This node is meant to capture molecular tests that were completed clinically for the participant and only includes data from diagnostic array that was completed prior to research sequencing was done. Do not include data related to research assay outputs here.
Id: TEXT | Unique identifier of entity e.g. a96059eb-81af-4b24-ae50-9242c0d8f819
Progression_or_Recurrence_Anatomic_Site: TEXT | The text term used to describe the anatomic site of resection; biopsy; tissue or organ of biospecimen origin; progression or recurrent disease; treatment
NCI_Atlas_Cancer_Site: TEXT | The primary tumor site used to calculate the incidence rate using the NCI Cancer Atlas, a digital atlas which provides geographical data related to cancer utilizing the Surveillance, Epidemiology, and End Results (SEER) Program cancer incidence rates for 2013 to 2017
Tissue_or_Organ_of_Origin: TEXT | The text term used to describe the anatomic site of origin, of the patient's malignant disease, as described by the World Health Organization's (WHO) International Classification of Diseases for Oncology (ICD-O).
Days_to_Last_Follow_up: TEXT | Time interval from the date of last follow up to the date of initial pathologic diagnosis, represented as a calculated number of days. If not applicable please enter 'Not Applicable'
Timepoint_Label: TEXT | Label to identify the time point at which the clinical data or biospecimen was obtained (e.g. Baseline, End of Treatment, Overall survival, Final). NO PHI/PII INFORMATION IS ALLOWED.
Days_to_Follow_Up: TEXT | Number of days between the date used for index and the date of the patient's last follow-up appointment or contact. If not applicable please enter 'Not Applicable'
Year_of_Death: TEXT | Numeric value to represent the year of the death of an individual.
Days_to_Progression: TEXT | Number of days between the date used for index and the date the patient's disease progressed. If not applicable please enter 'Not Applicable'
Primary_Diagnosis: TEXT | Text term used to describe the patient's histologic diagnosis, as described by the World Health Organization's (WHO) International Classification of Diseases for Oncology (ICD-O).
Days_to_Last_Known_Disease_Status: TEXT | Time interval from the date of last follow up to the date of initial pathologic diagnosis, represented as a calculated number of days. If not applicable please enter 'Not Applicable'
Tumor_Largest_Dimension_Diameter: TEXT | Numeric value used to describe the maximum diameter or dimension of the primary tumor, measured in centimeters.
Cancer_Incidence: TEXT | Incidence of specific cancer type in a defined area (a number between 0 and 100). The rate of incident cases per population of 100,000 persons of a specific type of cancer as designated in the "primary_diagnosis" data element in the county where the patient resides, using the most recent 2013-2017 NCI Cancer Atlas derived data.  Use patient zip code to find the county the patient lives in by going to https://www.unitedstateszipcodes.org/. Enter the zip code in the main text field and use the asociated county on the right side of the result field. On the https://gis.cancer.gov/canceratlas/tableview/ website, choose "Incidence" from the Topic dropdown menu, state of interest from the Area menu, "All Races" from the Race menu, and the cancer type ("Both Sexes" when possible) from the Statistic menu. Find the county of interest and enter the numeric Age-Adjusted Rate per 100,000 as the value.
Pack_Years_Smoked: TEXT | Numeric computed value to represent lifetime tobacco exposure defined as number of cigarettes smoked per day x number of years smoked divided by 20.
Stop_Days_from_Index: TEXT | Number of days from the date of birth (index date) to the end date of the event (e.g. exposure to environmental factor, treatment start, etc.). Note: if the event occurs at a single time point, e.g. a diagnosis or a lab test, the values for this column is 'Not Applicable'

Manifest_Id: TEXT | Synapse ID of manifest containing file annotation
HTAN_Parent_Data_File_ID: TEXT | HTAN Data File Identifier indicating the file(s) from which these files were derived
MS_Assay_Category: TEXT | Type of Mass Spectrometry performed.
Id: TEXT | Unique identifier of entity e.g. a96059eb-81af-4b24-ae50-9242c0d8f819
File_Size: NUMBER | Size of file (bucket object) in bytes
Filename: TEXT | Name of a file
HTAN_Parent_Biospecimen_ID: TEXT | HTAN Biospecimen Identifier (eg HTANx_yyy_zzz) indicating the biospecimen(s) from which these files were derived; multiple parent biospecimen should be comma-separated
File_Format: TEXT | Format of a file (e.g. txt, csv, fastq, bam, etc.)
HTAN_Data_File_ID: TEXT | Self-identifier for this data file - HTAN ID of this file HTAN ID SOP (eg HTANx_yyy_zzz)
md5: TEXT | md5 hash of file
Software_and_Version: TEXT | Name of software used to generate expression values. String
HTAN_Center: TEXT | Name of HTAN Center e.g. HTAN HTAPP
Data_Release: TEXT | Inclusion in HTAN Data Release e.g. Release 1.0
entityId: TEXT | Synapse ID of entity
Mass_Spectrometry_Auxiliary_File: TEXT | Auxiliary software parameter file used in mass spectrometry data processing, recorded as synapse ID (syn12345).
CDS_Release: TEXT | CDS transfer package in which file was included e.g. v22.6.1.seq
Component: TEXT | Category of metadata (e.g. Diagnosis, Biospecimen, scRNA-seq Level 1, etc.); provide the same one for all items/rows.
Manifest_Version: NUMBER | Latest version of metadata manifest
